---- dump tabulek a views
SELECT 
    c.TABLE_NAME,
    c.ORDINAL_POSITION                                AS poz,
    c.COLUMN_NAME,
    c.DATA_TYPE,
    c.CHARACTER_MAXIMUM_LENGTH                        AS delka,
    c.NUMERIC_PRECISION                               AS presnost,
    c.NUMERIC_SCALE                                   AS meritko,
    c.IS_NULLABLE                                     AS nullable,
    CASE WHEN pk.COLUMN_NAME IS NOT NULL THEN 'PK' ELSE '' END AS klic
FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS c
INNER JOIN INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES t
        ON t.TABLE_NAME = c.TABLE_NAME AND t.TABLE_SCHEMA = c.TABLE_SCHEMA
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT ku.TABLE_NAME, ku.COLUMN_NAME
    FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLE_CONSTRAINTS tc
    JOIN INFORMATION_SCHEMA.KEY_COLUMN_USAGE ku
            ON tc.CONSTRAINT_NAME = ku.CONSTRAINT_NAME
           AND tc.TABLE_NAME      = ku.TABLE_NAME
    WHERE tc.CONSTRAINT_TYPE = 'PRIMARY KEY'
) pk ON pk.TABLE_NAME = c.TABLE_NAME AND pk.COLUMN_NAME = c.COLUMN_NAME
WHERE t.TABLE_TYPE = 'BASE TABLE'
ORDER BY c.TABLE_NAME, c.ORDINAL_POSITION;

----

SELECT 
    s.name        AS schema_name,
    v.name        AS view_name,
    m.definition  AS create_script
FROM sys.views v
JOIN sys.schemas s ON s.schema_id = v.schema_id
JOIN sys.sql_modules m ON m.object_id = v.object_id
ORDER BY s.name, v.name;

dbo	qAgSKzPoh	CREATE VIEW [qAgSKzPoh] AS SELECT  SKzPoh.ID, SKzPoh.UsrOrder,SKzPoh.Sel, SKzPoh.Labels, SKzPoh.RelAg AS RelSKZpAg, SKzPoh.RelID, SKzPoh.RelIDV, SKzPoh.RefSKz, SKzPoh.RefUD, SKzPoh.OrderFld, SKz.RelSkTyp, SKz.RefSkSkup, SKz.RefStruct, SKz.RefSklad, SKz.IDS, SKz.EAN, SKz.Nazev, SKz.Nazev1, SKz.Nazev2, SKz.SText, SKz.MJ, SKzPoh.Zaruka, SKzPoh.RelZaruka, SKzPoh.RelOP, SKzPoh.Datum, SKzPoh.PohPMJ, SKzPoh.PohKc, SKzPoh.KcCelkem AS KcCelkemPoh, SKzPoh.KcOceneni, SKzPoh.VNakup, CAST(IsNull((SKzPoh.PohKc * SKzPoh.PohPMJ), 0) AS money) AS KcCelkemPol, CASE WHEN ((SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (5, 3, 6) OR (SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (0) AND SKzPoh.PohPMJ < 0))) THEN (SKzPoh.PohKc - SKzPoh.VNakup) ELSE (CAST(IsNull(0, 0) AS money)) END AS KcZisk, CAST(IsNull(CASE WHEN ((SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (5, 3, 6))) THEN (SKzPoh.PohKc * SKzPoh.PohPMJ - SKzPoh.KcCelkem) ELSE (CASE WHEN (((SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (0)) AND SKzPoh.PohPMJ < 0)) THEN ((ABS(SKzPoh.PohKc * SKzPoh.PohPMJ) - ABS(SKzPoh.KcCelkem))) ELSE (CAST(IsNull(0, 0) AS money)) END) END, 0) AS money) AS KcCZisk, CAST(CASE WHEN (SKzPoh.VNakup IS NULL OR SKzPoh.VNakup = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (((CASE WHEN ((SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (5, 3, 6) OR (SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (0) AND SKzPoh.PohPMJ < 0))) THEN (SKzPoh.PohKc - SKzPoh.VNakup) ELSE (CAST(IsNull(0, 0) AS money)) END / SKzPoh.VNakup) * 100)) END AS FLOAT) AS ZiskVNC, CAST(CASE WHEN (SKzPoh.PohKc IS NULL OR SKzPoh.PohKc = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (((CASE WHEN ((SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (5, 3, 6) OR (SKzPoh.OrderFld IN (0) AND SKzPoh.PohPMJ < 0))) THEN (SKzPoh.PohKc - SKzPoh.VNakup) ELSE (CAST(IsNull(0, 0) AS money)) END / SKzPoh.PohKc) * 100)) END AS FLOAT) AS ZiskPohKc, SKzPoh.StavZ, SKzPoh.SkUMD, SKzPoh.SkUD, SKzPoh.Cislo, SKzPoh.RefAD, SKzPoh.RefADdod, SKzPoh.Firma, SKzPoh.Jmeno, SKzPoh.ICO, SKzPoh.Obec, SKzPoh.RefZeme, SKzPoh.Firma2, SKzPoh.Jmeno2, SKzPoh.Obec2, SKzPoh.RefZeme2, SKzPoh.RefStr, SKzPoh.RefCin, SKzPoh.CisloZAK, SKzPoh.RefUcet, SKzPoh.RefRcPr, SKzPoh.STextRcPr, SKzPoh.KcRcPr, SKzPoh.MJRcPr, SKzPoh.MJKoefRcPr, SKzPoh.VCislo , SKzPoh.AUcet, SKz.RelSKzVC AS SKzSKzVC, SKz.RelSkDruh, SKz.Firma As SKzFirma, SKz.Vyrobce, SKzPoh.PolSKzVC, SKzPoh.DatExp, SKzPoh.Oznacil , NULL AS PzdAut  FROM SKz INNER JOIN SKzPoh ON SKz.ID = SKzPoh.RefSKz 
dbo	qCINpol	CREATE VIEW [qCINpol] AS SELECT sCIN.ID, qhCINpolG.RefGroup, qhCINpolG.RelCSZAg, qhCINpolG.OrdFldIDR, qhCINpolG.RelTpHO, qhCINpolG.RefAg, qhCINpolG.Datum, qhCINpolG.Cislo, qhCINpolG.Kc FROM sCIN INNER JOIN qhCINpolG ON qhCINpolG.RefGroup = sCIN.ID
dbo	qDPHShCheckNew	CREATE VIEW [qDPHShCheckNew] AS SELECT Max(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kod) AS Kod, Count(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.ID) AS Pocet, Max(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.DIC) AS DIC, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kc0) AS Kc0, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kc1) AS Kc1, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.KcDPH1) AS KcDPH1, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kc2) AS Kc2, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.KcDPH2) AS KcDPH2, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kc3) AS Kc3, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.KcDPH3) AS KcDPH3, Sum(DPHSHpodkladyTmp.KcCelkem) AS KcCelkem FROM DPHSHpodkladyTmp GROUP BY DPHSHpodkladyTmp.Kod, DPHSHpodkladyTmp.DIC
dbo	qDPHShCheckOld	CREATE VIEW [qDPHShCheckOld] AS SELECT Max(DPHSHpodklady.Kod) AS Kod, Count(DPHSHpodklady.ID) AS Pocet, Max(DPHSHpodklady.DIC) AS DIC, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.Kc0) AS Kc0, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.Kc1) AS Kc1, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.KcDPH1) AS KcDPH1, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.Kc2) AS Kc2, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.KcDPH2) AS KcDPH2, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.Kc3) AS Kc3, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.KcDPH3) AS KcDPH3, Sum(DPHSHpodklady.KcCelkem) AS KcCelkem FROM DPHSHpodklady WHERE (DPHSHpodklady.RefAg=222) GROUP BY DPHSHpodklady.Kod, DPHSHpodklady.DIC
dbo	qDPHzaok	CREATE VIEW [qDPHzaok] AS SELECT rpDPH1.ID AS ID , Sum(rpDPH1.Kc1) AS Kc1 , Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH1) AS KcDPH1 , Sum(rpDPH1.Kc2) AS Kc2 , Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH2) AS KcDPH2 , Sum(rpDPH1.Kc3) AS Kc3 , Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH3) AS KcDPH3 FROM rpDPH1 GROUP BY rpDPH1.ID HAVING (Sum(rpDPH1.Kc1) <> 0) OR (Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH1) <> 0) OR (Sum(rpDPH1.Kc2) <> 0) OR (Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH2) <> 0) OR (Sum(rpDPH1.Kc3) <> 0) OR (Sum(rpDPH1.KcDPH3) <> 0) 
dbo	qFAPolSlozZ	CREATE VIEW [qFAPolSlozZ] AS SELECT FApol.*,  (TbAddSlZ.SKcJednSum) AS SKcJedn , TbAddSlZ.SMnoz, CASE WHEN (FApol.Mnozstvi IS NULL OR FApol.Mnozstvi = 0) THEN (TbAddSlZ.SJCbezDPH) ELSE (TbAddSlZ.SJCbezDPH/FApol.Mnozstvi) END AS SJCbezDPH,   TbAddSlZ.SKc, TbAddSlZ.SKcDPH, (TbAddSlZ.SCmJednSum) AS SCmJedn, TbAddSlZ.SCm, TbAddSlZ.SCmDPH, TbAddSlZ.RelSzDPH AS RelSzDPHS, TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH AS ProcentoDPHS, TbAddSlZ.SDph AS SDphS, TbAddSlZ.PDP AS PDPS,  CASE WHEN ((FApol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ) AND (FApol.Mnozstvi <> 0) AND (((FApol.SDPH = TbAddSlZ.SDPH) AND (FApol.RelSzDPH = TbAddSlZ.RelSzDPH) AND (((FApol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL AND TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH IS NULL)) OR (FApol.ProcentoDPH = TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH))) OR (FApol.KcJedn = 0 AND FApol.Kc = 0 AND FApol.KcDPH = 0))) THEN (4) ELSE (CASE WHEN (TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ = FApol.RefParentZ AND FApol.RefParentZ <> FApol.ID AND FApol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND FApol.RefParentZ <> 0 AND (((TbRefParent.SDPHSlozZ = FApol.SDPH) AND (TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ = FApol.RelSzDPH) AND ((TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ IS NULL AND FApol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL) OR (TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ = FApol.ProcentoDPH))) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ > 0 AND TbRefParent.JeCastka = 0) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ = 0 AND TbAddSlZ.SKc = 0))) THEN (2) ELSE (CASE WHEN ((FApol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ AND (FApol.ID = FApol.RefParentZ OR FApol.RefParentZ IS NULL))) THEN (3) ELSE (CASE WHEN (FApol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND FApol.RefParentZ <> FApol.ID) THEN (1) ELSE (0) END) END) END) END AS RelTpPol , TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ, TbRefParent.JeCastka , CASE WHEN (CntGPol IS NULL OR CntGPol = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (SumSlevaPol/CntGPol) END AS SlevaGPol FROM (FApol LEFT JOIN (SELECT TbSlozZ.ID, CASE WHEN (TbSLozZ.RelSzDPH IS NULL) THEN (0) ELSE (TbSLozZ.RelSzDPH) END AS RelSzDPHSlozZ, TbSLozZ.ProcentoDPH AS ProcentoDPHSlozZ,CASE WHEN ((TbSlozZ.KcJedn = 0 AND TbSlozZ.KcDPH = 0 AND TbSlozZ.Kc = 0)) THEN (0) ELSE (1) END AS JeCastka, CASE WHEN (TbSlozZ.Mnozstvi Is NULL OR TbSlozZ.Mnozstvi = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (1) END AS JeMnozSlozZ, TbSlozZ.SDPH AS SDPHSlozZ , CASE WHEN ((TbSlozZ.Sleva Is NULL OR TbSlozZ.Sleva = 0)) THEN (0) ELSE (TbSlozZ.Sleva) END AS SlevaSlozZ FROM FApol AS TbSlozZ WHERE (RefParentZ IS NULL OR ID = RefParentZ) AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM FApol WHERE TbSlozZ.ID = FApol.RefParentZ AND FApol.RefParentZ <> FApol.ID)) AS TbRefParent ON FApol.RefParentZ = TbRefParent.ID)  LEFT JOIN ( SELECT TabGPol.*  FROM ( SELECT RefParentZ, COUNT(RefParentZ) AS CntNGPol FROM FApol WHERE RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND FApol.RefParentZ <> FApol.ID GROUP BY RefParentZ ) AS TabNGPol INNER JOIN ( SELECT RefParentZ, COUNT(RefParentZ) AS CntGPol, SUM(Mnozstvi) AS SMnoz,SUM(CASE WHEN (SDPH <> 0) THEN (Kc + KcDPH) ELSE (Kc) END) AS SKcJednSum,  SUM(Mnozstvi * JCbezDPH) AS SJCbezDPH,  SUM(Kc) AS SKc, SUM(KcDPH) AS SKcDPH, SUM(CASE WHEN (SDPH <> 0) THEN (Cm + CmDPH) ELSE (Cm) END) AS SCmJednSum, SUM(Cm) AS SCm, SUM(CmDPH) AS SCmDPH, RelSzDPH, ProcentoDPH, SDph , PDP , Sum(Sleva) AS SumSlevaPol FROM FApol INNER JOIN FA ON FApol.RefAg = FA.ID  WHERE (RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND FApol.RefParentZ <> FApol.ID AND ((FA.RelTpFak NOT IN (4, 6) AND STextRcPr IS NULL AND (MJKoefRcPr IS NULL OR MJKoefRcPr = 0)) OR (FA.RelTpFak IN (4, 6) AND RefParentZ IS NOT NULL)))  GROUP BY RefParentZ, RelSzDPH, ProcentoDPH, SDph , PDP ) AS TabGPol ON TabNGPol.RefParentZ = TabGPol.RefParentZ WHERE TabGPol.CntGPol = TabNGPol.CntNGPol ) AS TbAddSlZ ON (FApol.RefParentZ = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ OR FApol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ)

dbo	qHOPol	CREATE VIEW [qHOPol] AS SELECT HOpol.*, Kc AS KcCelk,  (TbAddSlZ.SKcJednSum) AS SKcJedn , TbAddSlZ.SMnoz, CASE WHEN (HOpol.Mnozstvi IS NULL OR HOpol.Mnozstvi = 0) THEN (TbAddSlZ.SJCbezDPH) ELSE (TbAddSlZ.SJCbezDPH/HOpol.Mnozstvi) END AS SJCbezDPH,   TbAddSlZ.SKc, TbAddSlZ.SKcDPH, (TbAddSlZ.SCmJednSum) AS SCmJedn, TbAddSlZ.SCm, TbAddSlZ.SCmDPH, TbAddSlZ.RelSzDPH AS RelSzDPHS, TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH AS ProcentoDPHS, TbAddSlZ.SDph AS SDphS, TbAddSlZ.PDP AS PDPS,  CASE WHEN ((HOpol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ) AND (HOpol.Mnozstvi <> 0) AND (((HOpol.SDPH = TbAddSlZ.SDPH) AND (HOpol.RelSzDPH = TbAddSlZ.RelSzDPH) AND (((HOpol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL AND TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH IS NULL)) OR (HOpol.ProcentoDPH = TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH))) OR (HOpol.KcJedn = 0 AND HOpol.Kc = 0 AND HOpol.KcDPH = 0))) THEN (4) ELSE (CASE WHEN (TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ = HOpol.RefParentZ AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> HOpol.ID AND HOpol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> 0 AND (((TbRefParent.SDPHSlozZ = HOpol.SDPH) AND (TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ = HOpol.RelSzDPH) AND ((TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ IS NULL AND HOpol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL) OR (TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ = HOpol.ProcentoDPH))) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ > 0 AND TbRefParent.JeCastka = 0) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ = 0 AND TbAddSlZ.SKc = 0))) THEN (2) ELSE (CASE WHEN ((HOpol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ AND (HOpol.ID = HOpol.RefParentZ OR HOpol.RefParentZ IS NULL))) THEN (3) ELSE (CASE WHEN (HOpol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> HOpol.ID) THEN (1) ELSE (0) END) END) END) END AS RelTpPol , TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ, TbRefParent.JeCastka , CASE WHEN (CntGPol IS NULL OR CntGPol = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (SumSlevaPol/CntGPol) END AS SlevaGPol FROM (HOpol LEFT JOIN (SELECT TbSlozZ.ID, CASE WHEN (TbSLozZ.RelSzDPH IS NULL) THEN (0) ELSE (TbSLozZ.RelSzDPH) END AS RelSzDPHSlozZ, TbSLozZ.ProcentoDPH AS ProcentoDPHSlozZ,CASE WHEN ((TbSlozZ.KcJedn = 0 AND TbSlozZ.KcDPH = 0 AND TbSlozZ.Kc = 0)) THEN (0) ELSE (1) END AS JeCastka, CASE WHEN (TbSlozZ.Mnozstvi Is NULL OR TbSlozZ.Mnozstvi = 0) THEN (0) ELSE (1) END AS JeMnozSlozZ, TbSlozZ.SDPH AS SDPHSlozZ , CASE WHEN ((TbSlozZ.Sleva Is NULL OR TbSlozZ.Sleva = 0)) THEN (0) ELSE (TbSlozZ.Sleva) END AS SlevaSlozZ FROM HOpol AS TbSlozZ WHERE (RefParentZ IS NULL OR ID = RefParentZ) AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM HOpol WHERE TbSlozZ.ID = HOpol.RefParentZ AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> HOpol.ID)) AS TbRefParent ON HOpol.RefParentZ = TbRefParent.ID)  LEFT JOIN ( SELECT TabGPol.*  FROM ( SELECT RefParentZ, COUNT(RefParentZ) AS CntNGPol FROM HOpol WHERE RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> HOpol.ID GROUP BY RefParentZ ) AS TabNGPol INNER JOIN ( SELECT RefParentZ, COUNT(RefParentZ) AS CntGPol, SUM(Mnozstvi) AS SMnoz,SUM(CASE WHEN (SDPH <> 0) THEN (Kc + KcDPH) ELSE (Kc) END) AS SKcJednSum,  SUM(Mnozstvi * JCbezDPH) AS SJCbezDPH,  SUM(Kc) AS SKc, SUM(KcDPH) AS SKcDPH, SUM(CASE WHEN (SDPH <> 0) THEN (Cm + CmDPH) ELSE (Cm) END) AS SCmJednSum, SUM(Cm) AS SCm, SUM(CmDPH) AS SCmDPH, RelSzDPH, ProcentoDPH, SDph , PDP , Sum(Sleva) AS SumSlevaPol FROM HOpol  WHERE (RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND HOpol.RefParentZ <> HOpol.ID AND STextRcPr IS NULL AND (MJKoefRcPr IS NULL OR MJKoefRcPr = 0))  GROUP BY RefParentZ, RelSzDPH, ProcentoDPH, SDph , PDP ) AS TabGPol ON TabNGPol.RefParentZ = TabGPol.RefParentZ WHERE TabGPol.CntGPol = TabNGPol.CntNGPol ) AS TbAddSlZ ON (HOpol.RefParentZ = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ OR HOpol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ)

<> 0) AND (((NABpol.SDPH = TbAddSlZ.SDPH) AND (NABpol.RelSzDPH = TbAddSlZ.RelSzDPH) AND (((NABpol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL AND TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH IS NULL)) OR (NABpol.ProcentoDPH = TbAddSlZ.ProcentoDPH))) OR (NABpol.KcJedn = 0 AND NABpol.Kc = 0 AND NABpol.KcDPH = 0))) THEN (4) ELSE (CASE WHEN (TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ = NABpol.RefParentZ AND NABpol.RefParentZ <> NABpol.ID AND NABpol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND NABpol.RefParentZ <> 0 AND (((TbRefParent.SDPHSlozZ = NABpol.SDPH) AND (TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ = NABpol.RelSzDPH) AND ((TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ IS NULL AND NABpol.ProcentoDPH IS NULL) OR (TbRefParent.ProcentoDPHSlozZ = NABpol.ProcentoDPH))) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ > 0 AND TbRefParent.JeCastka = 0) OR (TbRefParent.JeMnozSlozZ = 0 AND TbAddSlZ.SKc = 0))) THEN (2) ELSE (CASE WHEN ((NABpol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ AND (NABpol.ID = NABpol.RefParentZ OR NABpol.RefParentZ IS NULL))) THEN (3) ELSE (CASE WHEN (NABpol.RefParentZ IS NOT NULL AND NABpol.RefParentZ <> NABpol.ID) THEN (1) ELSE (0) END) END) END) END AS RelTpPol , TbRefParent.RelSzDPHSlozZ, TbRefParent.JeCastka , CASE WHEN (CntGPol IS NULL OR CntGPol = 0) THEN (0) ELSE RefParentZ, RelSzDPH, ProcentoDPH, SDph , PDP ) AS TabGPol ON TabNGPol.RefParentZ = TabGPol.RefParentZ WHERE TabGPol.CntGPol = TabNGPol.CntNGPol ) AS TbAddSlZ ON (SKPVpol.RefParentZ = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ OR SKPVpol.ID = TbAddSlZ.RefParentZ) 
dbo	qSKzVCpoh	CREATE VIEW [qSKzVCpoh] AS SELECT CAST(0 AS int) AS ID, CAST(0 AS int) AS RefVC, VCislo, RelID, RelIDV, RefSKz, 2025 AS Rok, Datum, RelSKZpAg, RelOP, Cislo, PohPMJ, Firma, Jmeno, OrderFld, Zaruka, RelZaruka FROM qAgSKzPoh WHERE (VCislo Is Not Null) AND (RefSKz Is Not Null) AND (SKzSKzVC<>0) AND (PolSKzVC<>0) UNION ALL SELECT CAST(0 AS int), RefVC, CAST('' AS VARCHAR), CAST(0 AS int), CAST(0 AS int), CAST(0 AS int), Rok, Datum, RelSKZpAg, RelOP, Cislo, PohPMJ, Firma, Jmeno, CAST(0 AS int), Zaruka, RelZaruka FROM SKzVChst WHERE (RefVC Is Not Null) UNION ALL SELECT SKzVCPoh.ID, 0, SKzVC.VCislo, CAST(0 AS int), CAST(0 AS int), SKzVCPoh.RefSKz, CAST(0 AS int), SKzVCPoh.Datum, CAST(0 AS int), SKzVCPoh.RelOP, CAST('' AS VARCHAR), SKzVCPoh.PohPMJ, CAST('' AS VARCHAR), CAST('' AS VARCHAR), CAST(0 AS int), NULL, NULL FROM SKzVCPoh INNER JOIN SKzVC ON SKzVCPoh.RefVC = SKzVC.ID WHERE (SKzVCPoh.RefVC Is Not Null) 
dbo	qSTRpol	CREATE VIEW [qSTRpol] AS SELECT sSTR.ID, qhSTRpolG.RefGroup, qhSTRpolG.RelCSZAg, qhSTRpolG.OrdFldIDR, qhSTRpolG.RelTpHO, qhSTRpolG.RefAg, qhSTRpolG.Datum, qhSTRpolG.Cislo, qhSTRpolG.Kc FROM sSTR INNER JOIN qhSTRpolG ON qhSTRpolG.RefGroup = sSTR.ID
dbo	qsZakPoh002	CREATE VIEW [qsZakPoh002] AS SELECT RelID, RefSkz, KcCelkem FROM SKzPoh WHERE (RelAg In (2))

dbo	qZavKcKRozd	CREATE VIEW [qZavKcKRozd] AS SELECT FA.ID AS FAID, Sum(IsNull(Uhrady.KcKRozd,0)) AS KcKRozdCelkem FROM FA INNER JOIN Uhrady ON FA.ID = Uhrady.RelIDH WHERE (FA.RefCM IS NOT NULL) AND (FA.RelStorn IS NULL) AND (FA.RelForUh IN (SELECT ID FROM sFormUh WHERE RelTyp = 3 AND BPUhr <> 0)) AND ((FA.RelTpFak In (11,2,13,14,15,16)) OR ((FA.RelTpFak = 8) AND (((FA.KcCelkem <=  0) AND (FA.TpStorn = 0)) OR ((FA.KcCelkem >= 0) AND (FA.TpStorn <> 0)))) OR ((FA.RelTpFak = 18) AND (((FA.KcCelkem > 0) AND (FA.TpStorn = 0)) OR ((FA.KcCelkem <  0) AND (FA.TpStorn <> 0)))) OR ((FA.RelTpFak = 1) AND ((FA.RefCM IS NULL AND FA.KcLikv < 0) OR (FA.RefCM IS NOT NULL AND FA.CmLikv < 0)) AND FA.TpStorn = 0)) AND (Uhrady.RelAgH IN (2,43,18,3,44,19)) GROUP BY FA.ID
